# And there we are, the 300th regular enemy! :)
# This 300th enemy also happens to be the first depth 50 enemy in the game. Because of this,
# we need to make a special monster to commemorate this event!

# At depth 21, you've seen the Firestorm Eagle, and ever since, you were wondering what
# happened to the Bird family. You assumed it just died, like Bats and Ants...
# And then all of a sudden, bam!! It has risen from it's ashes!

# Enters the Phoenix of Solar Flames.
# This legendary bird of fire is said to be able to revive from it's ashes. And here,
# the legend is quite true.

# The Phoenix of Solar Flames is a terrifying enemy, and is going to be the toughest
# foe you've faced so far. In terms of stats, only the Mature Dragons can compare.
# It is very rare, and you're not likely to encounter it on your
# first trip to depth 50. But if you do, think twice before facing it.

# It has a fire aura that also make fire fields. And it has a huge variety of melee and
# magic attacks. And worst part: it is immortal. How can you defeat such a foe? That's up
# to you to find out. ;)

# Good luck! :)

# The final boss of the Stealthy Vipers questline!
# Quite a difficult foe. This creature's versatility is scary, to say the least.
# It is capable of melee, ranged and magic attacks, has excellent resistances and
# is capable of summoning and teleporting. The two elemental weaknesses are made
# up for by having a high hp, excellent magic defense and very good AC, not to mention
# the "Block All" counters. It has Physical, Darkness, Toxic, Fire and Harm attacks, not
# to mention potentially more elements from summons.

# Jack-of-all-trades, master of all! A creature worthy of it's CR of 3, and a powerful
# final opponent for the Stealthy Vipers questline. Good luck! :)

# 2300+: Nightmare Horrors
# There is no limits to the deadliness, viciousness and cheapness of these monsters.
# Just know that you are entirely responsible for their appearence!

# As of 0.5, they have been further enhanced. These monsters are completely overpowered,
# imbalanced(in their favor, of course), cheap, and overall an unpleasant experience.
# Under most circumstances, you have to FLEE from the Nightmare!

# The first Nightmare is the Nightmare Scout.
# Based on Dark Familiar, this one is much, MUCH stronger. In fact, unless you find a way
# to prevent them from summoning things, you will very likely die. Quickly.

# Let's analyze this "scout" imp:
# - Beats a Boss Mature Prismatic Dragon in terms of stats.
# - Can summon copies of itself, which can summon copies of themselves.
# - Has extra lives.
# - Can pierce your resistances.

# And there you have it! The "weakest" of the Nightmare Horrors! :)

###### SCALED MONSTERS ######

# The signature monster type of Secret Levels, Scaled monsters are always 50% higher
# level than you. So if you're level 50, the will be level 75. If you're level 100,
# they will be level 150.

# Furthermore, they gain +1% to all their stats, skills, hp and ac modifiers every levels,
# in addition to getting "Boss" monsters modifiers as well. They often have a lot of powerful
# attacks, nasty tricks, and sometimes are actually very complex opponents.

#############################
###  THE ANCIENT DEMIGOD  ###
#############################

# As divine beings, they outclass mortals in every ways, with 200% modifiers across the board.
# Of course, it's a scaled enemy, and it will at LEAST have 275% modifiers because of that.
# Make it CR4, the ability to recover 20% hp every turns, and you have one powerful foe. 
# But this is amongst the nicest enemies you will encounter in secret levels. :)
N:2500:Corrupted Divine Guard
G:A:W
I:140:200:20:200:0:0:0:0:0:0:0:0:4
W:75:1:1700:0
B:200:200:200:200:0:200:200:200:6:0:1:20:0:0
E:1:1:1:2:1:1
C:19:100

A:hit:Halberd:1:6d10:15:0:0:1:11:1:6

A:hit:Flame Strike:1:6d10:1:0:0:1:11:1:6
A:hit:Gust Strike:1:6d10:10:0:0:1:11:1:6

D:Divine Guards are upper celestial beings that lives in the planes of demigods and other 
D:immortal beings, and are part of those commonly known as Divine Champions. Although they 
D:are low rank Divine Champions, they outclass most mortals in every ways, in both body and 
D:mind, as well as other lesser celestials. They rarely appear in the mortal world except 
D:in times of great peril. However, in this plane, the Divine Guards have been corrupted 
D:by some evil force. They are now twisted and evil, and will not hesitate to use their 
D:immense power to cause death and destruction. This corrupted winged warrior wields a 
D:powerful blessed halberd, and wields incredibly powerful magic of light and wind. Thanks 
D:to his immortal life force, wounds that do not destroy him will heal extremely quickly.
